    /*
     * Initialize the local Turbo instance.
     *
     * "buffer" can be an ArrayBuffer or SharedArrayBuffer.  In the
     * latter case, all workers must pass the same buffer during
     * initialization.
     *
     * The buffer must be zero-initialized before being passed to
     * init().  Turbo assumes ownership of the buffer, client code
     * should not access it directly after using it to initialize
     * the heap.
     *
     * "start" must be a valid offset within the buffer, it is the
     * first byte that may be used.
     *
     * "limit" must be a valid offset within the buffer, limit-1 is
     * the last byte that may be used.
     *
     * "initialize" must be true in exactly one agent and that call
     * must return before any agent can call any other methods on
     * their local Turbo objects.  Normally, you would allocate your
     * memory in the main thread, call Turbo.init(buffer, true) in
     * the main thread, and then distribute the buffer to workers.
     */
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype.init = function (buffer, start, limit, initialize) {
        Iif (arguments.length < 3) {

        }
        start = (start + 7) & ~7;
        limit = (limit & ~7);
        Iif (start < 0 || limit <= start || limit > buffer.byteLength) {

        Iif (len < 16) {

        this._mem_int16 = new Int16Array(buffer, start, len / 2);
        this._mem_uint16 = new Uint16Array(buffer, start, len / 2);

    };
    /*

    };
    /*
     * Given an pointer to a class instance, return its type object.
     * Return null if no type object is found.
     */
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype.identify = function (p) {
        if (p == 0)
            return null;
        if (this._idToType.hasOwnProperty(this._mem_int32[p >> 2]))
            return this._idToType[this._mem_int32[p >> 2]];
        return null;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._badType = function (self) {
        var t = this.identify(self);
        return new Error("Observed type: " + (t ? t.NAME : "*invalid*") + ", address=" + self);
    };
    // Synchronic layout is 8 bytes (2 x int32) of metadata followed by
    // the type-specific payload.  The two int32 words are the number
    // of waiters and the wait word (generation count).
    //
    // In the following:
    //
    // self is the base address for the Synchronic.
    // mem is the array to use for the value
    // idx is the index in mem of the value: (p+8)>>log2(mem.BYTES_PER_ELEMENT)
    //
    // _synchronicLoad is just Atomics.load, expand it in-line.
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicStore = function (self, mem, idx, value) {
        Atomics.store(mem, idx, value);
        this._notify(self);
        return value;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicCompareExchange = function (self, mem, idx, oldval, newval) {
        var v = Atomics.compareExchange(mem, idx, oldval, newval);
        if (v == oldval)
            this._notify(self);
        return v;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicAdd = function (self, mem, idx, value) {
        var v = Atomics.add(mem, idx, value);
        this._notify(self);
        return v;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicSub = function (self, mem, idx, value) {
        var v = Atomics.sub(mem, idx, value);
        this._notify(self);
        return v;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicAnd = function (self, mem, idx, value) {
        var v = Atomics.and(mem, idx, value);
        this._notify(self);
        return v;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicOr = function (self, mem, idx, value) {
        var v = Atomics.or(mem, idx, value);
        this._notify(self);
        return v;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicXor = function (self, mem, idx, value) {
        var v = Atomics.xor(mem, idx, value);
        this._notify(self);
        return v;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicLoadWhenNotEqual = function (self, mem, idx, value) {
        for (;;) {
            var tag = Atomics.load(this._mem_int32, (self + 4) >> 2);
            var v = Atomics.load(mem, idx);
            if (v !== value)
                break;
            this._waitForUpdate(self, tag, Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY);
        }
        return v;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicLoadWhenEqual = function (self, mem, idx, value) {
        for (;;) {
            var tag = Atomics.load(this._mem_int32, (self + 4) >> 2);
            var v = Atomics.load(mem, idx);
            if (v === value)
                break;
            this._waitForUpdate(self, tag, Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY);
        }
        return v;
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._synchronicExpectUpdate = function (self, mem, idx, value, timeout) {
        var now = this._now();
        var limit = now + timeout;
        for (;;) {
            var tag = Atomics.load(this._mem_int32, (self + 4) >> 2);
            var v = Atomics.load(mem, idx);
            if (v !== value || now >= limit)
                break;
            this._waitForUpdate(self, tag, limit - now);
            now = this._now();
        }
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._waitForUpdate = function (self, tag, timeout) {
        // Spin for a short time before going into the futexWait.
        //
        // Hard to know what a good count should be - it is machine
        // dependent, for sure, and "typical" applications should
        // influence the choice.  If the count is high without
        // hindering an eventual drop into futexWait then it will just
        // decrease performance.  If the count is low it is pointless.
        // (This is why Synchronic really wants a native implementation.)
        //
        // Data points from a 2.6GHz i7 MacBook Pro:
        //
        // - the simple send-integer benchmark (test-sendint.html),
        //   which is the very simplest case we can really imagine,
        //   gets noisy timings with an iteration count below 4000
        //
        // - the simple send-object benchmark (test-sendmsg.html)
        //   gets a boost when the count is at least 10000
        //
        // 10000 is perhaps 5us (CPI=1, naive) and seems like a
        // reasonable cutoff, for now - but note, it is reasonable FOR
        // THIS SYSTEM ONLY, which is a big flaw.
        //
        // The better fix might well be to add some kind of spin/nanosleep
        // functionality to futexWait, see https://bugzil.la/1134973.
        // That functionality can be platform-dependent and even
        // adaptive, with JIT support.
        var i = 10000;
        do {
            // May want this to be a relaxed load, though on x86 it won't matter.
            if (Atomics.load(this._mem_int32, (self + 4) >> 2) != tag)
                return;
        } while (--i > 0);
        Atomics.add(this._mem_int32, self >> 2, 1);
        Atomics.futexWait(this._mem_int32, (self + 4) >> 2, tag, timeout);
        Atomics.sub(this._mem_int32, self >> 2, 1);
    };
    RuntimeConstructor.prototype._notify = function (self) {
        Atomics.add(this._mem_int32, (self + 4) >> 2, 1);
        // Would it be appropriate & better to wake n waiters, where n
        // is the number loaded in the load()?  I almost think so,
        // since our futexes are fair.
        if (Atomics.load(this._mem_int32, self >> 2) > 0)
            Atomics.futexWake(this._mem_int32, (self + 4) >> 2, Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY);
    };
    return RuntimeConstructor;
}());
exports.RuntimeConstructor = RuntimeConstructor;
exports.turbo = {
    Runtime: new RuntimeConstructor()
};

// For allocators: Do not round up nbytes, for now.  References to
// fields within structures can be to odd addresses and there's no
// particular reason that an object can't be allocated on an odd
// address.  (Later, with a header or similar info, it will be
// different.)
// Note, actual zero-initialization is not currently necessary
// since the buffer must be zero-initialized by the client code
// and this is a simple bump allocator.
function alloc_sab(nbytes, alignment) {
    do {
        var p = Atomics.load(this._mem_int32, 1);
        var q = (p + (alignment - 1)) & ~(alignment - 1);
        var top = q + nbytes;
        Iif (top >= this._mem_int32[2])
            return 0;
    } while (Atomics.compareExchange(this._mem_int32, 1, p, top) != p);
    return q;
}
function alloc_ab(nbytes, alignment) {
    var p = this._mem_int32[1];
    p = (p + (alignment - 1)) & ~(alignment - 1);
    var top = p + nbytes;
    if (top >= this._mem_int32[2])
        return 0;
    this._mem_int32[1] = top;
    return p;
}

function fract(f) {
    return f - Math.floor(f);
}
function fract_add1(f) {
    var f1 = f - Math.floor(f);
    return f1 - Math.floor(f1 + 1);
}
function clampInt(x, lo, hi) {
    if (x < lo) {
        return lo;
    }
    if (x > hi) {
        return hi;
    }
    return x;
}

    Color.Kelvin = function (K) {
        var red;
        var green;
        var blue;
        // red
        if (K >= 6600) {
            var A = 351.97690566805693;
            var B = 0.114206453784165;
            var c = -40.25366309332127;
            var x = K / 100 - 55;
            red = A + B * x + c * Math.log(x);
        }
        else {
            red = 255;
        }
        // green
        if (K >= 6600) {
            A = 325.4494125711974;
            B = 0.07943456536662342;
            c = -28.0852963507957;

            green = A + B * x + c * Math.log(x);
        }
        else if (K >= 1000) {
            A = -155.25485562709179;
            B = -0.44596950469579133;
            c = 104.49216199393888;

    Vector.MinAxis = function (a) {
        var x = Math.abs(a.X);
        var y = Math.abs(a.Y);
        var z = Math.abs(a.Z);
        if (x <= y && x <= z) {
            return xyz(1, 0, 0);
        }
        else if (y <= x && y <= z) {
            return xyz(0, 1, 0);
        }
        return xyz(0, 0, 1);
    };
    Vector.MinAxis_mem = function (a, c) {

            y = 0;
            z = 0;
        }

            x = 0;
            y = 1;
            z = 0;
        }
        else {
            x = 0;
            y = 0;
            z = 1;
        }
        if (c) {
            exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(c + 8) >> 3] = x;
            exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(c + 16) >> 3] = y;

    Vector.Refract = function (a, b, n1, n2) {
        var nr = n1 / n2;
        var cosI = -Vector.Dot(a, b);
        var sinT2 = nr * nr * (1 - cosI * cosI);
        if (sinT2 > 1) {
            return xyz(0, 0, 0);
        }
        var cosT = Math.sqrt(1 - sinT2);
        return Vector.Add(Vector.MulScalar(b, nr), Vector.MulScalar(a, nr * cosI - cosT));
    };
    Vector.Refract_mem = function (a, b, n1, n2, c) {
        var nr = n1 / n2;
        var cosI = -Vector.Dot_mem(a, b);
        var sinT2 = nr * nr * (1 - cosI * cosI);
        if (sinT2 > 1) {
            return Vector.Init_mem(Vector.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(32, 8)));
        }
        var cosT = Math.sqrt(1 - sinT2);
        c = c ? c : Vector.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(32, 8));
        return Vector.Add_mem(Vector.MulScalar_mem(b, nr), Vector.MulScalar_mem(a, nr * cosI - cosT, c), c);
    };
    Vector.Reflectance = function (a, b, n1, n2) {
        var nr = n1 / n2;
        var cosI = -Vector.Dot(a, b);
        var sinT2 = nr * nr * (1 - cosI * cosI);
        if (sinT2 > 1) {
            return 1;
        }
        var cosT = Math.sqrt(1 - sinT2);
        var rOrth = (n1 * cosI - n2 * cosT) / (n1 * cosI + n2 * cosT);
        var rPar = (n2 * cosI - n1 * cosT) / (n2 * cosI + n1 * cosT);
        return (rOrth * rOrth + rPar * rPar) / 2;
    };
    Vector.Reflectance_mem = function (a, b, n1, n2) {
        var nr = n1 / n2;
        var cosI = -Vector.Dot_mem(a, b);
        var sinT2 = nr * nr * (1 - cosI * cosI);
        if (sinT2 > 1) {
            return 1;
        }
        var cosT = Math.sqrt(1 - sinT2);
        var rOrth = (n1 * cosI - n2 * cosT) / (n1 * cosI + n2 * cosT);
        var rPar = (n2 * cosI - n1 * cosT) / (n2 * cosI + n1 * cosT);
        return (rOrth * rOrth + rPar * rPar) / 2;
    };

        return exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 8) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 16) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 24) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 32) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 32) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 40) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 48) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 56) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 64) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 64) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 72) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 72) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 80) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 80) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 88) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 88) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 96) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 96) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 104) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 104) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 112) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 112) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 120) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 120) >> 3] && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 128) >> 3] == exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 128) >> 3];
    };
    Matrix.IsIdentity = function (a) {
        return exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 8) >> 3] == 1 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 16) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 24) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 32) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3] == 1 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 64) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 72) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 80) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 88) >> 3] == 1 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 96) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 104) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 112) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 120) >> 3] == 0 && exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 128) >> 3] == 1;
    };
    Matrix.TranslateUnitMatrix = function (v, c) {
        var ptr = c ? c : Matrix.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(136, 8));
        return Matrix.init(ptr, 1, 0, 0, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3], 0, 1, 0, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3], 0, 0, 1, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3], 0, 0, 0, 1);
    };
    Matrix.ScaleUnitMatrix = function (v, c) {
        var ptr = c ? c : Matrix.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(136, 8));
        return Matrix.init(ptr, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3], 0, 0, 0, 0, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3], 0, 0, 0, 0, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3], 0, 0, 0, 0, 1);
    };
    Matrix.RotateUnitMatrix = function (v, a, _c) {
        v = Vector.Normalize_mem(v);
        var s = Math.sin(a);
        var c = Math.cos(a);
        var m = 1 - c;
        var ptr = _c ? _c : Matrix.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(136, 8));
        return Matrix.init(ptr, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3] + c, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3] * s, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3] - exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3] * s, 0, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3] - exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3] * s, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3] + c, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3] * s, 0, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3] * s, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 16) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3] - exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 8) >> 3] * s, m * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(v + 24) >> 3] + c, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1);
    };
    Matrix.FrustumUnitMatrix = function (l, r, b, t, n, f, c) {
        var t1 = 2 * n;
        var t2 = r - l;
        var t3 = t - b;
        var t4 = f - n;
        var ptr = c ? c : Matrix.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(136, 8));
        return Matrix.init(ptr, t1 / t2, 0, (r + l) / t2, 0, 0, t1 / t3, (t + b) / t3, 0, 0, 0, (-f - n) / t4, (-t1 * f) / t4, 0, 0, -1, 0);
    };
    Matrix.OrthographicUnitMatrix = function (l, r, b, t, n, f, c) {
        var ptr = c ? c : Matrix.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(136, 8));
        return Matrix.init(ptr, 2 / (r - l), 0, 0, -(r + l) / (r - l), 0, 2 / (t - b), 0, -(t + b) / (t - b), 0, 0, -2 / (f - n), -(f + n) / (f - n), 0, 0, 0, 1);
    };
    Matrix.PerspectiveUnitMatrix = function (fovy, aspect, near, far, c) {
        var ymax = near * Math.tan(fovy * Math.PI / 360);
        var xmax = ymax * aspect;
        return Matrix.Frustum(-xmax, xmax, -ymax, ymax, near, far, c);
    };
    Matrix.LookAtMatrix = function (eye, center, up, c) {
        up = Vector.Normalize_mem(up);
        var f = Vector.Normalize_mem(Vector.Sub_mem(center, eye));
        var s = Vector.Normalize_mem(Vector.Cross_mem(f, up));
        var u = Vector.Cross_mem(s, f);
        var ptr = c ? c : Matrix.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(136, 8));
        Matrix.init(ptr, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(s + 8) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(u + 8) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(f + 8) >> 3], 0, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(s + 16) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(u + 16) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(f + 16) >> 3], 0, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(s + 24) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(u + 24) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(f + 24) >> 3], 0, 0, 0, 0, 1);
        return Matrix.Translate(Matrix.Inverse(Matrix.Transpose(ptr, ptr), ptr), eye, ptr);
    };
    Matrix.Translate = function (m, v, c) {
        return Matrix.Mul(m, Matrix.TranslateUnitMatrix(v), c);
    };
    Matrix.Scale = function (m, v) {
        return Matrix.Mul(m, Matrix.ScaleUnitMatrix(v));
    };
    Matrix.Rotate = function (m, v, a) {
        return Matrix.Mul(m, Matrix.RotateUnitMatrix(v, a));
    };
    Matrix.Frustum = function (m, l, r, b, t, n, f) {
        return Matrix.Mul(m, Matrix.FrustumUnitMatrix(l, r, b, t, n, f));
    };
    Matrix.Orthographic = function (m, l, r, b, t, n, f) {
        return Matrix.Mul(m, Matrix.OrthographicUnitMatrix(l, r, b, t, n, f));
    };
    Matrix.Perspective = function (m, fovy, aspect, near, far) {
        return Matrix.Mul(m, Matrix.PerspectiveUnitMatrix(fovy, aspect, near, far));
    };
    Matrix.Mul = function (a, b, m) {
        m = m ? m : Matrix.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(136, 8));
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 8) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 8) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 16) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 40) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 24) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 72) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 32) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 104) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 40) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 40) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 72) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 64) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 104) >> 3];

        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 48) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 48) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 80) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 64) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 112) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 80) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 72) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 80) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 48) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 88) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 80) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 96) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 112) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 112) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 104) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 112) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 48) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 120) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 80) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 128) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 112) >> 3];

        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 56) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 56) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 88) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 64) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 120) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 88) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 72) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 80) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 56) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 88) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 88) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 96) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 120) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 120) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 104) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 112) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 56) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 120) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 88) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 128) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 120) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 32) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 8) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 32) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 16) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 64) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 24) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 96) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 32) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 128) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 64) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 32) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 64) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 96) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 64) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 128) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 96) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 72) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 32) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 80) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 64) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 88) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 96) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 96) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 128) >> 3];
        exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(m + 128) >> 3] = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 104) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 32) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 112) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 64) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 120) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 96) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 128) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 128) >> 3];
        return m;
    };
    Matrix.MulPosition = function (a, b, c) {
        var x = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 8) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 16) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 24) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 32) >> 3];
        var y = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 64) >> 3];
        var z = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 72) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 80) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 88) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 96) >> 3];
        var ptr = c ? c : Vector.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(32, 8))();
        return Vector.Init_mem(ptr, x, y, z);
    };
    Matrix.MulDirection = function (a, b, c) {
        var x = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 8) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 16) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 24) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3];
        var y = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3];
        var z = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 72) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 8) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 80) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 16) >> 3] + exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 88) >> 3] * exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(b + 24) >> 3];
        var ptr = c ? c : Vector.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(32, 8))();
        return Vector.Normalize_mem(Vector.Init_mem(ptr, x, y, z));
    };
    Matrix.MulRay = function (a, b) {
        return ray(Matrix.MulPosition(a, b.Origin), Matrix.MulDirection(a, b.Direction));
    };
    Matrix.MulBox = function (a, box, c) {
        var min = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_int32[(box + 4) >> 2];
        var max = exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_int32[(box + 8) >> 2];
        // http://dev.theomader.com/transform-bounding-boxes/
        var r = Vector.Init_mem(Vector.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(32, 8)), exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 8) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 40) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 72) >> 3]);
        var u = Vector.Init_mem(Vector.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(32, 8)), exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 16) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 48) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 80) >> 3]);
        var b = Vector.Init_mem(Vector.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(32, 8)), exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 24) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 56) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 88) >> 3]);
        var t = Vector.Init_mem(Vector.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(32, 8)), exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 32) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 64) >> 3], exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(a + 96) >> 3]);
        var xa = Vector.MulScalar_mem(r, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(min + 8) >> 3]);
        var xb = Vector.MulScalar_mem(r, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(max + 8) >> 3]);
        var ya = Vector.MulScalar_mem(u, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(min + 16) >> 3]);
        var yb = Vector.MulScalar_mem(u, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(max + 16) >> 3]);
        var za = Vector.MulScalar_mem(b, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(min + 24) >> 3]);
        var zb = Vector.MulScalar_mem(b, exports.turbo.Runtime._mem_float64[(max + 24) >> 3]);
        xa = Vector.Min_mem(xa, xb, r);
        xb = Vector.Max_mem(xa, xb, u);
        ya = Vector.Min_mem(ya, yb, b);
        yb = Vector.Max_mem(ya, yb);
        za = Vector.Min_mem(za, zb);
        zb = Vector.Max_mem(za, zb);
        min = Vector.Add_mem(Vector.Add_mem(Vector.Add_mem(xa, ya), za), t);
        max = Vector.Add_mem(Vector.Add_mem(Vector.Add_mem(xb, yb), zb), t);
        var ptr = c ? c : Box.initInstance(exports.turbo.Runtime.allocOrThrow(12, 4));
        return Box.Init_mem(ptr, min, max);
    };
